<img alt="" class="intrinsic-content" height="220" loading="lazy" sizes="(max-width: 47.9375em) 100vw, 25vw" src="https://i1.wp.com/www.nationalreview.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/fbi-small.jpg?resize=380%2C220&amp;ssl=1" srcset="https://i1.wp.com/www.nationalreview.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/fbi-small.jpg?resize=300%2C175&amp;ssl=1 300w, https://i1.wp.com/www.nationalreview.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/fbi-small.jpg?resize=140%2C80&amp;ssl=1 140w, https://i1.wp.com/www.nationalreview.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/fbi-small.jpg?resize=380%2C220&amp;ssl=1 380w, https://i1.wp.com/www.nationalreview.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/fbi-small.jpg?resize=50%2C29&amp;ssl=1 50w, https://i1.wp.com/www.nationalreview.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/fbi-small.jpg?zoom=2&amp;resize=380%2C220&amp;ssl=1 760w" width="380"/> </a>
</figure>
